评论人：photosofbritain
评论时间：2018-02-03
评论内容：Would you rather go wild camping or stay in a posh country hotel? I'm skint, sadly, so camping in the Lake District, Cumbria would be my pick! How gorgeous is this English countryside shot by @christographer.owens? This glorious vista is from Loughrigg Fell above Ambleside toward the northern end of Lake Windermere and Waterhead, Cumbria. . The @lake.district is where England's scenery takes an unexpected walk on the wild side. Nowhere in the nation packs such an instant panoramic punch: rivers rush, forces tumble, lakes glisten and lonely fells loom along an ever reaching horizon. But the @Lake.District is much more than just epic views. It's an historic textbook, a rural heartland, a foodie heaven, an outdoor playground and a literary landmark all rolled into one breathtakingly beautiful scenic bundle. . And of course - this is Beatrix Potter land. Growing up, I loved reading the adventures of Peter Rabbit, Squirrel Nutkin and Jemima Puddle-Duck to name but a few. Potter holidayed as a child in the Lake District and was inspired by the flora, fauna and landscape, which she observed closely and painted. With the proceeds from her books, Potter bought ‘Hill Top Farm’ in Near Sawrey and over the following decades, purchased additional farms to preserve the unique hill country landscape. Potter wrote 30 books in all, the most famous being ‘The tale of Peter Rabbit’. Following her death in 1943, she left almost all of her property to the National Trust. What a truly wonderful woman. . If you want to see more stunning shots from this part of England, head over to my dedicated @lake.district hub! Lovely shot by @christographer.owens 🇬🇧 Want your Photos of Britain to be featured? Follow us and then add the tag #photosofbritain and tag us in the picture too! 🇬🇧

评论人：meetcutelondon
评论时间：2017-11-28
评论内容：第一次參加朋友小孩的雙滿月啪踢，吃到朋友媽媽親手作的油飯與麻油雞，在場其他朋友直呼：「有媽媽在身邊好好噢～」 首先說這件事我其實不太講，甚至可能很多長大以後才認識的朋友也都不知道，也許也是因為爸爸不喜歡我提的關係，記得很小的時候他就會說：「沒有媽媽不用讓全世界都知道」，所以最好是不要讓他知道我在這邊大聲嚷嚷比較好。 在倫敦遇到其他台灣人的時候，大部分的人都會問：「來多久了呀？」「那妳有其他兄弟姊妹嗎？」「哇！妳是獨生女，爸媽不會捨不得嗎？」問到這裡，我通常都也只是說「我爸都說出國就像丟掉，所以也不太管我的。」這時候就會出現兩種可能，一是可能發現我不是太有興趣繼續這個話題而轉移話題的人，二是完全沒感受到我的尷尬而繼續追問：「那妳媽媽呢？媽媽怎麼可能捨得女兒這麼久不回台灣的！？」 說實話的結果就是，「啊，對不起，我不知道，不好意思......」的尷尬收場。自己一個人在倫敦，這麼多年以來也該練就一番知道如何好好應對這些棘手問題的功夫，所以儘管尷尬，但其實我倒也不會有被冒犯到的感覺，畢竟也真的不是對方的錯，所以也沒什麼好說對不起的。但是昨天朋友一呼「有媽真好」，當下倒是讓我心裡一驚。 回家以後，我又陷入這個永遠不會有解答的問題漩渦：「如果媽媽在的話，我會是什麼樣的我呢？」 如果媽媽在的話，我應該在十八歲那年交換學生結束後，就不會再回來英國，乖乖在台灣把五專念畢業了吧。但隨即轉念一想，不對，如果媽媽在，她應該根本不會讓我去念五專而是要我走一般的教育體制念高中、升大學的。嗯，可是我根本沒考上高中啊，還是說，有媽媽在我就不會在國中的時候成績一落千丈，而是可以考上國立高中呢？她會讓我在高二休學一年出國當交換學生嗎？還是要等到大學畢業以後（如果我考得上大學的話），她才會讓我出國唸書呢？念完書是不是就得立刻回台灣了呢？ 回到殘酷的現實，我不知道我現在走的這條路比較好或是比較不好，也不知道如果媽媽看到現在的我，會不會支持我走上了這條通往英國的路。很多時候會覺得過去的自己一直是完全沒有考慮退路的往前衝，因此把現在自己逼倒一個無法回頭，而未來也還很遙遠的絕境。覺得自己在成長的過程中，因為沒有媽媽的指引和陪伴，從小就擁有極大自由的我（這點要感謝爸爸）很可能在自己摸索的途中犯了很多無法彌補的錯誤，走上設定以外的路程，但是幾乎百分之九十九都是我的選擇，實在無法怪罪任何人，必須自己為自己的人生負責。 總之，哀哀叫完以後還是要自己爬起來，沒到盡頭以前這條路還是要自己走下去。 最後再一次感謝朋友媽媽讓我們吃到糯米是特別從台灣扛來英國的油飯，吃完還讓我們包了便當回家，實在太感動了🙏😭

评论内容：⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀ 🇬🇧 Photo: @dan.thwaites 🇬🇧 _______________________________________ Good evening from the beautiful Lake District National Park, Cumbria, England! It's been a wonderful, unexpectedly sunny evening here in northern England... so what a superb shot to end today. Nothing finer than the glorious British countryside in my opinion. It's also a good excuse to plug our sister page @lake.district where there are oodles more pictures like this from Cumbria. I always think of the wonderful Beatrix Potter who was so influenced by this beautiful landscape when I visit. I grew up reading about Peter Rabbit, Jemima Puddle-Duck and friends, whilst skipping rocks in the lakes. Beatrix Potter herself spent many childhood holidays in the Lake District, and with the proceeds from the books and a legacy from an aunt, in 1905 Potter bought Hill Top Farm in Near Sawrey, a village in the Lake District. Over the following decades, she purchased additional farms to preserve the unique hill country landscape. Potter was also a prize-winning breeder of Herdwick sheep and a prosperous farmer keenly interested in land preservation. It's fair to say without her, this land would look very different. She saved so many farms and the views we take for granted today. A wonderfully influential woman, way ahead of her time. Super shot by @dan.thwaites 🇬🇧 Want your Photos of Britain to be featured? Follow us and then add the tag #photosofbritain and tag us in the picture too! 🇬🇧
